Order of the segments in a URL.\\n556: # Each list entry is a tuple of (path name (string), getter, setter).\\n557: # Note that the getters must not use FullyDecoded decoded mode to prevent loss\\n558: # of information. (host and path use FullyDecoded by default)\\n559: _URL_SEGMENTS = [\\n560:     (\\n561:         'host',\\n562:         lambda url: url.host(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\\n563:         lambda url, host: url.setHost(host, QUrl.StrictMode)),\\n564:     (\\n565:         'port',\\n566:         lambda url: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',\\n567:         lambda url, x: url.setPort(int(x))),\\n568:     (\\n569:         'path',\\n570:         lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\\n571:         lambda url, path: url.setPath(path, QUrl.StrictMode)),\\n572:     (\\n573:         'query',\\n574:         lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\\n575:         lambda url, query: url.setQuery(query, QUrl.StrictMode)),\\n576:     (\\n577:         'anchor',\\n578:         lambda url: url.fragment(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\\n579:         lambda url, fragment: url.setFragment(fragment, QUrl.StrictMode)),\\n580: ]\\n581: \\n582: \\n583: def incdec_number(url, incdec, count=1, segments=None):\\n584:     \\\"\\\"\\\"Find a number in the url and increment or decrement it.\\n585: \\n586:     Args:\\n587:         url: The current url\\n588:         incdec: Either 'increment' or 'decrement'\\n589:         count: The number to increment or decrement by\\n590:         segments: A set of URL segments to search. %3A = colon (:), followed by a real number\n        # The regex should find the real number 10, not the 3 or A in %3A\n        url = QUrl('http://localhost/path/%3A10')\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        expected = QUrl('http://localhost/path/%3A11')\n        assert result == expected, (\n            f\"Expected {expected.toString()}, got {result.toString()}\"\n        )\n\n    # ========================================================================\n    # BUG 2: Negative values are allowed\n    # ========================================================================\n\n    def test_decrement_below_zero_raises_error(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing below 0 raises an error, not produces negative.\"\"\"\n        # %C3%A4 is the UTF-8 encoding for 'ä' (a with umlaut)\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/path%C3%A4/page5')\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        expected = QUrl('http://example.com/path%C3%A4/page6')\n        assert result == expected, (\n            f\"Expected {expected.toString()}, got {result.toString()}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_mixed_encoded_and_plain_text(self):\n        \"\"\"Test paths with mixed encoded and plain text.\"\"\"\n        # The number 10 should be incremented, not any digits in encoded sequences\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/some%20path/10')\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        expected = QUrl('http://example.com/some%20path/11')\n        assert result == expected, (\n            f\"Expected {expected.toString()}, got {result.toString()}\"\n        )\n\n    # ========================================================================\n    # Additional edge cases related to the bugs\n    # ========================================================================\n\n    def test_percent_encoded_number_not_matched(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that digits in percent-encoded sequences are not matched.\n\n        For example, in %35 (encoded '5'), the 5 should not be incremented.\n        The negative lookbehind in the regex should prevent this.\n        \"\"\"\n        # %35 = '5', followed by a real number 10\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/%3510')\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        expected = QUrl('http://example.com/%3511')\n        assert result == expected, (\n            f\"Expected {expected.toString()}, got {result.toString()}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_no_number_in_encoded_sequences_only(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that a URL with only encoded sequences (no real numbers) raises error.\"\"\"\n        # %C3%B6 is 'ö' (o with umlaut), no actual numbers\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/%C3%B6/file')\n        with pytest.raises(urlutils.IncDecError) as exc_info:\n            urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        assert \"No number found\" in str(exc_info.value)\n\n    def test_encoded_percent_sign_followed_by_number(self):\n        \"\"\"Test handling of encoded percent sign %25 followed by a number.\n\n        %25 is the encoding for '%'. If we have %2510, this is '%10' encoded.\n        When decoded with PrettyDecoded, this might become '%10', which could\n        confuse the regex lookbehind.\n        \"\"\"\n        # This is an edge case: %25 is '%', so %2510 is '%10' encoded\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/%2510')\n        # Order of the segments in a URL.\\n556: # Each list entry is a tuple of (path name (string), getter, setter).\\n557: # Note that the getters must not use FullyDecoded decoded mode to prevent loss\\n558: # of information. (host and path use FullyDecoded by default)\\n559: _URL_SEGMENTS = [\\n560:     (\\n561:         'host',\\n562:         lambda url: url.host(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\\n563:         lambda url, host: url.setHost(host, QUrl.StrictMode)),\\n564:     (\\n565:         'port',\\n566:         lambda url: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',\\n567:         lambda url, x: url.setPort(int(x))),\\n568:     (\\n569:         'path',\\n570:         lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\\n571:         lambda url, path: url.setPath(path, QUrl.StrictMode)),\\n572:     (\\n573:         'query',\\n574:         lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\\n575:         lambda url, query: url.setQuery(query, QUrl.StrictMode)),\\n576:     (\\n577:         'anchor',\\n578:         lambda url: url.fragment(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\\n579:         lambda url, fragment: url.setFragment(fragment, QUrl.StrictMode)),\\n580: ]\\n581: \\n582: \\n583: def incdec_number(url, incdec, count=1, segments=None):\\n584:     \\\"\\\"\\\"Find a number in the url and increment or decrement it.\\n585: \\n586:     Args:\\n587:         url: The current url\\n588:         incdec: Either 'increment' or 'decrement'\\n589:         count: The number to increment or decrement by\\n590:         segments: A set of URL segments to search. Encoded sequences are corrupted when incrementing/decrementing\n2. Negative values are allowed instead of raising errors\n3. URL-encoded data is improperly decoded and lost\n\nThe tests are self-contained and include a minimal implementation of the\nbuggy incdec_number function for testing purposes.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport re\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtCore import QUrl\n\n\nclass IncDecError(Exception):\n    \"\"\"Exception raised by incdec_number on problems.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, msg, url):\n        super().__init__(msg)\n        self.url = url\n        self.msg = msg\n\n    def __str__(self):\n        return '{}: {}'.format(self.msg, self.url.toString())\n\n\ndef _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count):\n    \"\"\"Get an incremented/decremented URL based on a URL match.\"\"\"\n    pre, zeroes, number, post = match.groups()\n    val = int(number)\n    if incdec == 'decrement':\n        if val < count:\n            raise IncDecError(\"Can't decrement {} by {}!\".format(val, count), url)\n        val -= count\n    elif incdec == 'increment':\n        val += count\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(\"Invalid value {} for incdec!\".format(incdec))\n    if zeroes:\n        if len(number) < len(str(val)):\n            zeroes = zeroes[1:]\n        elif len(number) > len(str(val)):\n            zeroes += '0'\n    return ''.join([pre, zeroes, str(val), post])\n\n\n_URL_SEGMENTS = [\n    ('host', lambda url: url.host(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n     lambda url, host: url.setHost(host, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    ('port', lambda url: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',\n     lambda url, x: url.setPort(int(x))),\n    ('path', lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n     lambda url, path: url.setPath(path, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    ('query', lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n     lambda url, query: url.setQuery(query, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    ('anchor', lambda url: url.fragment(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n     lambda url, fragment: url.setFragment(fragment, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n]\n\n\ndef incdec_number(url, incdec, count=1, segments=None):\n    \"\"\"\n    BUGGY IMPLEMENTATION - This is the original buggy code from qutebrowser.\n\n    Find a number in the url and increment or decrement it.\n    This implementation has three main bugs:\n    1. Uses PrettyDecoded mode which decodes some percent-encoded sequences,\n       then tries to use regex lookbehinds as if they were still encoded\n    2. Allows negative numbers instead of properly rejecting them\n    3. Loses URL-encoded data through improper decode/encode cycle\n    \"\"\"\n    if not url.isValid():\n        raise ValueError(\"Invalid URL\")\n\n    if segments is None:\n        segments = {'path', 'query'}\n\n    url = QUrl(url)\n    for segment, getter, setter in reversed(_URL_SEGMENTS):\n        if segment not in segments:\n            continue\n\n        # BUG: The regex with negative lookbehind doesn't work correctly\n        # with PrettyDecoded because some sequences are already decoded\n        match = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)',\n                             getter(url))\n        if not match:\n            continue\n\n        setter(url, _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count))\n        return url\n\n    raise IncDecError(\"No number found in URL!\", url)\n\n\nclass TestIncDecNumberRegressions:\n    \"\"\"Regression tests for incdec_number bugs.\"\"\"\n\n    # ========================================================================\n    # BUG 1: Encoded sequences are corrupted or not properly handled\n    # ========================================================================\n\n    def test_encoded_colon_with_number_after(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that %3A (colon) followed by a number is handled correctly.\n\n        When incrementing http://localhost/%3A5, the result should be\n        http://localhost/%3A6, not corrupting the %3A encoding.\n\n        BUG: Because %3A is decoded to ':' with PrettyDecoded, and the\n        regex lookbehind doesn't prevent matching the subsequent number,\n        this might fail or produce unexpected results.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl('http://localhost/%3A5')\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        expected = QUrl('http://localhost/%3A6')\n        assert result == expected, (\n            f\"Expected {expected.toString()}, got {result.toString()}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_encoded_colon_in_query(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that %3A in query strings is preserved.\"\"\"\n        url = QUrl('http://localhost/page?param=%3A5')\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'query'})\n        expected = QUrl('http://localhost/page?param=%3A6')\n        assert result == expected, (\n            f\"Expected {expected.toString()}, got {result.toString()}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_encoded_colon_in_anchor(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that %3A in anchors is preserved.\"\"\"\n        url = QUrl('http://localhost/page#%3A5')\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'anchor'})\n        expected = QUrl('http://localhost/page#%3A6')\n        assert result == expected, (\n            f\"Expected {expected.toString()}, got {result.toString()}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_multiple_encoded_sequences_with_numbers(self):\n        \"\"\"Test URL with multiple encoded sequences containing digit-like chars.\"\"\"\n        # %3A = colon (:), followed by a real number\n        # The regex should find the real number 10, not the 3 or A in %3A\n        url = QUrl('http://localhost/path/%3A10')\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        expected = QUrl('http://localhost/path/%3A11')\n        assert result == expected, (\n            f\"Expected {expected.toString()}, got {result.toString()}\"\n        )\n\n    # ========================================================================\n    # BUG 2: Negative values are allowed (check validation logic)\n    # ========================================================================\n\n    def test_decrement_below_zero_raises_error(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing below 0 raises an error, not produces negative.\"\"\"\n        # Decrementing 1 by 2 should raise an error\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/page_1')\n        with pytest.raises(IncDecError) as exc_info:\n            incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=2, segments={'path'})\n        assert \"Can't decrement\" in str(exc_info.value)\n\n    def test_decrement_zero_by_one_raises_error(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing 0 by 1 raises an error.\"\"\"\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/page_0')\n        with pytest.raises(IncDecError) as exc_info:\n            incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=1, segments={'path'})\n        assert \"Can't decrement\" in str(exc_info.value)\n\n    def test_decrement_by_large_count_raises_error(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing by a large count raises an error.\"\"\"\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/page_5')\n        with pytest.raises(IncDecError) as exc_info:\n            incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=10, segments={'path'})\n        assert \"Can't decrement\" in str(exc_info.value)\n\n    def test_decrement_exact_to_zero_succeeds(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing exactly to 0 succeeds (edge case).\"\"\"\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/page_5')\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=5, segments={'path'})\n        expected = QUrl('http://example.com/page_0')\n        assert result == expected, (\n            f\"Expected {expected.toString()}, got {result.toString()}\"\n        )\n\n    # This is the original buggy code from qutebrowser.\n\n    Find a number in the url and increment or decrement it.\n    This implementation has three main bugs:\n    1. Uses PrettyDecoded mode which decodes some percent-encoded sequences,\n       then tries to use regex lookbehinds as if they were still encoded\n    2. Allows negative numbers instead of properly rejecting them\n    3. Loses URL-encoded data through improper decode/encode cycle\n    \"\"\"\n    if not url.isValid():\n        raise ValueError(\"Invalid URL\")\n\n    if segments is None:\n        segments = {'path', 'query'}\n\n    url = QUrl(url)\n    for segment, getter, setter in reversed(_URL_SEGMENTS):\n        if segment not in segments:\n            continue\n\n        # BUG: The regex with negative lookbehind doesn't work correctly\n        # with PrettyDecoded because some sequences are already decoded\n        match = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)',\n                             getter(url))\n        if not match:\n            continue\n\n        setter(url, _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count))\n        return url\n\n    raise IncDecError(\"No number found in URL!\", url)\n\n\nclass TestIncDecNumberRegressions:\n    \"\"\"Regression tests for incdec_number bugs.\"\"\"\n\n    #
